In 2002, the airport in Lennon's home town was renamed the <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_John_Lennon_Airport" title="Liverpool John Lennon Airport">Liverpool John Lennon Airport</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fola_255-0"><a href="#cite_note-fola-255"><span>[</span>255<span>]</span></a></sup> In 2010, on what would have been Lennon's 70th birthday, the <a href="/wiki/John_Lennon_Peace_Monument" title="John Lennon Peace Monument">John Lennon Peace Monument</a> was unveiled in <a href="/wiki/Chavasse_Park" title="Chavasse Park">Chavasse Park</a>, Liverpool, by Cynthia and Julian Lennon.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-256"><a href="#cite_note-256"><span>[</span>256<span>]</span></a></sup> The sculpture entitled 'Peace &amp; Harmony' exhibits <a href="/wiki/Peace_symbols" title="Peace symbols">peace symbols</a> and carries the inscription "Peace on Earth for the Conservation of Life · In Honour of John Lennon 1940–1980".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-257"><a href="#cite_note-257"><span>[</span>257<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Marx-Lennon_Abkhazia_stamp.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1220" data-file-width="1600" height="229" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/Marx-Lennon_Abkhazia_stamp.jpg/300px-Marx-Lennon_Abkhazia_stamp.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/Marx-Lennon_Abkhazia_stamp.jpg/450px-Marx-Lennon_Abkhazia_stamp.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/Marx-Lennon_Abkhazia_stamp.jpg/600px-Marx-Lennon_Abkhazia_stamp.jpg 2x" width="300"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Marx-Lennon_Abkhazia_stamp.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Groucho_Marx" title="Groucho Marx">Groucho Marx</a> and Lennon on a 1994 <a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Abkhazia</a> stamp parodying <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Marxism-Leninism" title="Marxism-Leninism">Marxism-Leninism</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In December 2013 the <a href="/wiki/International_Astronomical_Union" title="International Astronomical Union">International Astronomical Union</a> named one of the craters on <a href="/wiki/Mercury_(planet)" title="Mercury (planet)">Mercury</a> after Lennon.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-258"><a href="#cite_note-258"><span>[</span>258<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Awards_and_sales">Awards and sales</span></h3>
<div class="hatnote boilerplate seealso">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_the_Beatles" title="List of awards and nominations received by the Beatles">List of awards and nominations received by the Beatles</a></div>
<p>The Lennon–McCartney songwriting partnership is regarded as one of the most influential and successful of the 20th century. As performer, writer or co-writer Lennon has had 25 number one singles on the US <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Hot_100" title="Billboard Hot 100">Hot 100</a> chart.<sup class="reference plainlinks nourlexpansion" id="ref_fn_a"><a href="#endnote_fn_a">a</a></sup> His album sales in the US stand at 14 million units.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTERIAA2010b_259-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTERIAA2010b-259"><span>[</span>259<span>]</span></a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/Double_Fantasy" title="Double Fantasy">Double Fantasy</a></i> was his best-selling solo album,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEGreenberg2010202_260-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEGreenberg2010202-260"><span>[</span>260<span>]</span></a></sup> at three million shipments in the US;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTERIAA2010a_261-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTERIAA2010a-261"><span>[</span>261<span>]</span></a></sup> Released shortly before his death, it won the 1981 <a href="/wiki/Grammy_Award_for_Album_of_the_Year" title="Grammy Award for Album of the Year">Grammy Award for Album of the Year</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEgrammy.com_262-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEgrammy.com-262"><span>[</span>262<span>]</span></a></sup> The following year, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BRIT_Awards" title="BRIT Awards">BRIT Award</a> for Outstanding Contribution to Music went to Lennon.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEBrit_Awards2010_263-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEBrit_Awards2010-263"><span>[</span>263<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>Participants in a 2002 BBC poll voted him eighth of "<a href="/wiki/100_Greatest_Britons" title="100 Greatest Britons">100 Greatest Britons</a>".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEBBC_News2002_264-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEBBC_News2002-264"><span>[</span>264<span>]</span></a></sup> Between 2003 and 2008, <i><a href="/wiki/Rolling_Stone" title="Rolling Stone">Rolling Stone</a></i> recognised Lennon in several reviews of artists and music, ranking him fifth of "100 Greatest Singers of All Time"<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEBrowne2008_265-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEBrowne2008-265"><span>[</span>265<span>]</span></a></sup> and 38th of "100 Greatest Artists of All Time",<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTERolling_Stone2008_266-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTERolling_Stone2008-266"><span>[</span>266<span>]</span></a></sup> and his albums <i><a href="/wiki/John_Lennon/Plastic_Ono_Band" title="John Lennon/Plastic Ono Band">John Lennon/Plastic Ono Band</a></i> and <i>Imagine</i>, 22nd and 76th respectively of "<a href="/wiki/Rolling_Stone%27s_500_Greatest_Albums_of_All_Time" title="Rolling Stone's 500 Greatest Albums of All Time">Rolling Stone's 500 Greatest Albums of All Time</a>".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTERolling_Stone2008_266-1"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTERolling_Stone2008-266"><span>[</span>266<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTERolling_Stone2003_267-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTERolling_Stone2003-267"><span>[</span>267<span>]</span></a></sup> He was appointed <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_British_Empire" title="Order of the British Empire">Member of the Order of the British Empire (MBE)</a> with the other Beatles in 1965 (returned in 1969<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-268"><a href="#cite_note-268"><span>[</span>268<span>]</span></a></sup>).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTELondon_Gazette19655488_269-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTELondon_Gazette19655488-269"><span>[</span>269<span>]</span></a></sup> Lennon was posthumously inducted into the <a href="/wiki/Songwriters_Hall_of_Fame" title="Songwriters Hall of Fame">Songwriters Hall of Fame</a> in 1987<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTESongwriters_Hall_of_Fame2009_270-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTESongwriters_Hall_of_Fame2009-270"><span>[</span>270<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources#What_information_to_include" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources"><span title="A more detailed citation is required. (December 2014)">full citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> and into the <a href="/wiki/Rock_and_Roll_Hall_of_Fame" title="Rock and Roll Hall of Fame">Rock and Roll Hall of Fame</a> in 1994.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEThe_Rock_and_Roll_Hall_of_Fame_and_Museum1994_110-1"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEThe_Rock_and_Roll_Hall_of_Fame_and_Museum1994-110"><span>[</span>110<span>]</span></a></sup><br/></p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span></h2>
<div class="refbegin" style="">
<p><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_fn_a"><b><a href="#ref_fn_a">^ Note a:</a></b></span> Lennon was responsible for 25 <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Hot_100" title="Billboard Hot 100"><i>Billboard</i> Hot 100</a> number one singles as performer, writer or co-writer.</p>
<ul>
<li>Solo (2): "<a href="/wiki/Whatever_Gets_You_thru_the_Night" title="Whatever Gets You thru the Night">Whatever Gets You thru the Night</a>", "<a href="/wiki/(Just_Like)_Starting_Over" title="(Just Like) Starting Over">(Just Like) Starting Over</a>".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEAllmusic2010a_271-0"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEAllmusic2010a-271"><span>[</span>271<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>With The Beatles (20): "<a href="/wiki/Can%27t_Buy_Me_Love" title="Can't Buy Me Love">Can't Buy Me Love</a>", "<a href="/wiki/I_Feel_Fine" title="I Feel Fine">I Feel Fine</a>", "<a href="/wiki/I_Want_to_Hold_Your_Hand" title="I Want to Hold Your Hand">I Want to Hold Your Hand</a>", "<a href="/wiki/Love_Me_Do" title="Love Me Do">Love Me Do</a>", "<a href="/wiki/She_Loves_You" title="She Loves You">She Loves You</a>", "<a href="/wiki/A_Hard_Day%27s_Night_(song)" title="A Hard Day's Night (song)">A Hard Day's Night</a>", "<a href="/wiki/Eight_Days_a_Week" title="Eight Days a Week">Eight Days a Week</a>", "<a href="/wiki/Help!_(song)" title="Help!
